### [219] [GroundControl: Anticipating Navigation Failures in Vision-Language Agents via Trajectory-Consistent Uncertainty Estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20479)
*Nastaran Darabi,Divake Kumar,Sina Tayebati,Devashri Naik,Amit Ranjan Trivedi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于视觉-语言导航（VLN）任务的新不确定性评估方法 GroundControl，用于提前预测导航失败风险，并通过新的评价协议展示了其显著优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉-语言导航智能体在平均表现上已很优异，但在实际执行时仍容易陷入轨迹级的失败（如停滞、振荡或绕远）。现有的不确定性信号多只捕捉即时行动的模糊性，难以提前捕捉整体失败风险，影响了系统部署的可靠性。

Method: GroundControl 使用轨迹一致性的不确定性估计，将任务进行时的距目标距离随时间的动态建模（利用常速Kalman滤波），根据偏离理想动态的统计量并结合轨迹整体特征（如推进性、单调性、路径效率、振荡行为）计算全局不确定性分数。此外提出SRCN评估协议，引入风险-覆盖曲线和AURC/E-AURC指标独立测量不确定性排序好坏。

Result: 在5个导航分组下，GroundControl 在成功率风险排序方面接近理想排序，表现显著优于基于熵、共形和启发式方法，并在多模型和分组下持续取得最低AURC/E-AURC指标。

Conclusion: 通过建模与目标导向动态的偏离，GroundControl 能提供可解释且鲁棒的不确定性信号，实现提前预警视觉-语言导航失败，有望增强实际应用的可靠性。

Abstract: Vision-language navigation agents achieve competitive average success on benchmark tasks, yet failures often arise through predictable trajectory-level breakdowns such as oscillation, stagnation, or inefficient detours. Reliable deployment, therefore, requires uncertainty signals that anticipate emerging failure dynamics during execution rather than reflect only instantaneous action entropy. We introduce \emph{GroundControl}, a trajectory-consistent uncertainty estimator defined as statistical deviation from nominal goal-directed distance-to-goal dynamics aggregated over an episode. GroundControl models distance evolution using a constant-velocity Kalman filter and combines normalized innovation statistics with complementary trajectory features capturing progress, monotonicity, path efficiency, and oscillatory behavior. The resulting uncertainty score reflects geometric and temporal inconsistency in navigation behavior rather than local prediction dispersion. To evaluate uncertainty quality independently of task success, we formalize \emph{Selective Risk--Coverage Navigation (SRCN)}, a protocol that measures how effectively an uncertainty score ranks episodes by failure or inefficiency using risk--coverage curves and AURC / E-AURC summaries. Across five EB-Navigation splits ($N=300$ episodes), trajectory-consistent uncertainty achieves near-oracle ordering under success-based selective risk, with weighted-average $\mathrm{E\text{-}AURC}_{\mathrm{SR}}=0.0024$ for the GPT-4o model, substantially outperforming entropy-, conformal-, and heuristic baselines. Under SPL-based selective evaluation, GroundControl consistently achieves the lowest AURC and E-AURC across models and navigation splits. These results show that modeling deviation from goal-directed dynamics provides an interpretable and robust signal for anticipating navigation failures in vision-language agents.

</details>

It outperforms existing recurrent baselines across diverse evaluation metrics, while reducing computational costs by 99.40% and accelerating inference by up to six times. To investigate the role of human attention modeling in robot autonomy and demonstrate the practical utility of this highly efficient architecture, we integrate GazeLNN into an active camera-robot control policy trained via Reinforcement Learning. ### [221] [Increasing Resilience of Continuum Robots via Motion Planning Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20495)
*Oxana Shamilyan,Ievgen Kabin,Zoya Dyka,Oleksandr Sudakov,Peter Langendoerfer*

TL;DR: 该论文实验性研究了提高连续体机器人抗损能力的运动规划方法，重点分析了多准则决策如何影响路径规划和执行效率。通过引入层次分析法（AHP）评估路径质量，对比了遗传算法和A star算法，结果显示遗传算法生成的路径多样且对环境规模不敏感，有助于提升机器人抗损性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用遗传算法和A star两种常用路径规划算法，加入层次分析法评估和加权四项准则（距离、电机损坏、机械臂损坏、精度），在两种仿真环境中分别测试算法表现，并比对路径多样性及执行效率。

Result: 实验表明遗传算法生成的路径在种类上显著多于A star，且受环境复杂度影响较小，执行时间稳定；A star执行时间则随环境规模增加而增大。多准则决策能提升路径的多样性，从而增强机器人抗损能力。

Conclusion: 将多准则决策引入路径规划能提升连续体机器人在实际应用中的鲁棒性和耐久性。遗传算法结合层次分析法表现出较强的抗环境复杂度性能，适合用于需要高抗损性的连续体机器人运动规划。

Abstract: This paper presents an experimental study of motion planning for resilient continuum robots. In this study we mainly focused on multi-criteria decision-making, its application for path-planning algorithms, impact on the generated path and execution time. To do this, we used two well-known algorithms for path planning, namely Genetic algorithm and A star algorithm, and modified them by adding the Analytical Hierarchy Process algorithm to evaluate the quality of the paths generated. In our experiment the Analytical Hierarchy Process considers four different criteria, i.e. distance, motors damage, mechanical damage of the robot's arm and accuracy, each considered to contribute to the resilience of a continuum robot. The use of different criteria is necessary to increase the time to maintenance operations of the continuum robot. We conducted the experiments using two different simulated environments of the robot. Although we significantly simplified the robot's model and its environment, we still implemented some of the features of the environment based on the real robot prototype. In particular, one of the environments has single- as well as multi-path points, and other consists of the multi-path points only. The results show that, in contrast to A star, the performance time of Genetic algorithm does not depend on the environment's cardinality. It generates more diverse paths, which increases the robot's resilience.

</details>


### [222] [Generating Robot Hands from Human Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20549)
*Sha Yi,Nicklas Hansen,Xueqian Bai,Carmelo Sferrazza,Michael T. Tolley,Xiaolong Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于人类演示数据的数据驱动框架，用于自动生成可通过简单控制实现复杂任务的机器人手结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前机器人控制学习进展迅速，但物理结构（如机械手）的学习设计依然困难，因为需要联合优化设计和控制，导致搜索空间极大，难以求解。需要新方法简化该过程。

Method: 收集和使用人类日常操作中超过400万帧指尖运动数据，使用逆运动学算法生成机器人手结构，使其能通过相同、简单的控制策略（仅配合指尖位置）完成目标动作。引入强化学习方法加速结构与关节角度的搜索优化，同时实现机械手一体化3D打印。

Result: 提出的框架能自动生成兼具通用性与专用性的机器人手，包括6自由度多功能机械手和多种特定任务用的低自由度手结构。6自由度机械手在真机实验中其远程操作性能超过市售机械手。低自由度版本以简化结构实现了对特定运动的高效再现。设计搜索速度从数小时缩短到数分钟。

Conclusion: 大规模人类运动数据不仅能训练机器人控制器，也能成为优化和生成机器人物理结构的新依据，实现设计与控制的有效分离和加速，推动机器人硬件智能化。

Abstract: Robot learning has advanced rapidly in learning control, but learning the physical body of a robot remains much more difficult because jointly searching over design and control creates a very large combinatorial problem. Here, we present a data-driven framework for generating robot hands from human demonstrations. Instead of learning a complex controller together with each candidate design, we generate robot hand designs using the same simple control policy used after fabrication: matching fingertip positions through inverse kinematics. Using more than 4 million frames of human fingertip motion from everyday manipulation, our algorithm optimizes tree-structured robot hands to reproduce desired target motions. The framework produced both a 6-degree-of-freedom (DoF) general-purpose hand and lower-DoF task-specific hands with spatial four-bar mimic joints. To accelerate the search over designs, we trained a reinforcement-learning (RL) actor to propose good hand designs and joint angles, reducing search time from hours to minutes. We fabricated the mechanisms directly as one-piece articulated structures with print-in-place joints. In real-world experiments, the 6-DoF hand achieved highly accurate teleoperated fingertip tracking better than available commercial robot hands, whereas the specialized 3-DoF hands reproduced structured human and synthetic trajectories with reduced mechanical complexity. These results showed that large-scale human motion data can be used not only to train robot controllers but also as a reference for optimizing and generating the physical embodiment of robots.

</details>


### [223] [MemoryWAM: Efficient World Action Modeling with Persistent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20562)
*Sizhe Yang,Juncheng Mu,Tianming Wei,Chenhao Lu,Xiaofan Li,Linning Xu,Zhengrong Xue,Zhecheng Yuan,Dahua Lin,Jiangmiao Pang,Huazhe Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了MemoryWAM，一种具有效率持久记忆的世界动作模型，有效提升了机器人在长时序操控任务中的表现，并降低了推理延迟和计算资源消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的世界动作模型（WAMs）在效率和长时记忆之间存在权衡，导致在需要长期记忆的非马尔可夫环境下效果不佳，亟需一种既能有效保留历史信息又兼具推理效率的模型。

Method: MemoryWAM采用混合记忆设计，结合近期帧、事件边界锚帧与压缩的特征摘要token，并用定制化注意力机制，从而高效检索短期细节和长期压缩信息。

Result: MemoryWAM在多项需要长期记忆的操控任务（包含仿真与真实场景）中，相较于主流VLA与WAM基线方法表现更佳，同时保持了较低的延迟和GPU内存消耗。

Conclusion: MemoryWAM有效解决了长期历史与高效推理的矛盾，为现实环境下的机器人操控带来了更强的记忆力与更高的计算效率。

Abstract: Robust robotic manipulation in the real world requires not only an understanding of the current observation, but also memory and dynamics modeling. World action models (WAMs) possess these capabilities by jointly modeling visual foresight and actions conditioned on both current and historical observations, making them a promising paradigm for robotic manipulation. However, existing WAMs face a fundamental trade-off: methods with efficient inference typically condition only on a bounded window of recent observations and therefore struggle in non-Markovian environments, whereas methods that preserve long histories incur time and space costs that grow substantially with sequence length. To address this challenge, we introduce MemoryWAM, a world action model with efficient persistent memory. MemoryWAM uses a hybrid memory design that combines recent frames, event-boundary anchor frames, and compact gist tokens that summarize long-range history. A tailored attention mechanism enables retrieval of both detailed short-term context and compressed long-term context, supporting memory-dependent decision-making with reduced inference latency and GPU memory usage. Across long-horizon, memory-dependent manipulation tasks in both simulation and the real world, MemoryWAM outperforms strong vision-language-action (VLA) and WAM baselines while maintaining favorable computational efficiency.

</details>


### [224] [Human Universal Grasping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17054)
*Kevin Yuanbo Wu,Tianxing Zhou,Isaac Tu,Billy Yan,Irmak Guzey,David Fouhey,Dandan Shan,Lerrel Pinto*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了HUG模型，通过学习和模拟人类抓取操作，实现多指机器人对新物体的高效抓取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类具备很强的通用抓取能力，而多指机器人在这方面仍然存在很大差距。作者认为，人类的数据是最自然的机器人抓取数据来源，借此推动机器人抓取能力提升。

Method: 作者首先通过智能眼镜采集了包含1百万帧的人类抓取数据集（1M-HUGs）；随后提出一种全新的基于流匹配（flow-matching）的模型，融合RGB和深度信息，输出包括腕部位置、朝向和手部姿态（MANO）的抓取方案。预测出的抓取方式可以迁移到不同类型的机器人手上，实现零样本抓取。此外，作者还构建了包含90个新物体的标准化评测基准（HUG-Bench）。

Result: HUG模型在多个真实世界场景下以及自建的HUG-Bench评测基准上显著优于现有主流抓取算法，对困难物体集准确率提升了23%和34%。

Conclusion: 通过大规模人类抓取数据和创新性模型方法，能够显著提升多指机器人在复杂场景下的抓取能力。提出的评测基准为后续研究提供了标准化比较平台。

Abstract: Humans can grasp objects effortlessly, whereas multi-fingered robots are far from this level of generality. We argue that the most natural source of robot grasping data is from humans, who pick up thousands of objects every day. We present HUG, a flow-matching model that generates diverse human grasps for any user-specified object in a single RGB-D image captured from a stereo camera. Using smart glasses, we first collect 1M-HUGs, an egocentric dataset of human grasps spanning 1M frames (27.8 hrs) and 6,707 object instances across 41 buildings. Next, to model the distribution of natural human grasps, our novel flow-matching model fuses RGB and depth observations to output a grasp parameterized by wrist translation, wrist rotation, and MANO hand pose. Predicted grasps can be retargeted to various robot hands, enabling zero-shot grasping in everyday scenes. To standardize evaluation, we build a new simulated benchmark, HUG-Bench, of 90 unseen objects from five geometric categories and various sizes, with metric-scale 3D meshes. We evaluate HUG in the real world on the 30-object test set of HUG-Bench across multiple stereo cameras, robot embodiments, and household environments. HUG outperforms the state-of-the-art grasping baselines by +23% and +34% on our challenging object set. Code, data, benchmark, checkpoints, and an interactive demo are released on our website: https://grasping.io/

</details>
